Sports News

Chinese and British Main Players Compete for the Billiards Championship, Li Gongying vs. Glean, Zhang Yingda vs. Shekharm; the Chinese team lost a total of 250 points in the first three games; please look to the efforts of the main players. There is still hope for the championship.

In the Sino-British international billiards competition, the British players won all three of the previous games, for a total of 250 points. Today, the final two games between the second and first-ranked players from China and Britain will be held at the Victoria General Association at 5:30 PM and 9:00 PM respectively. Zhang Yingda of China was originally scheduled to play against Bowder of Britain, but he has been replaced by Shekharm. The first-ranked Li Gongying will play against Glean in the last game. There is no doubt that Li Gongying and Zhang Yingda, the main players of the Chinese team, will win. How much they win will be the key to this year's Sino-British championship.

Ding Mingyi Lost by One Shot

In yesterday's first game, Ding Mingyi of China played against Bolger of Britain. The situation was fairly even. Bolger continued to make two shots of 30 and 72, leading Ding by 100 points. Ding did not lose heart and focused on improving, gradually reducing the difference. Fortunately, the god of luck arrived, and he scored 46 and then 48, making the score 347. Since then, although he often fell behind, the number was very small. After 500 points, Ding suddenly made an incredible shot, causing the audience and Li Baying, the billiards king of Shanghai, to applaud and stick out their tongues. He accumulated 73 points in one hand, for a total of 575 points. At that time, he had surpassed his opponent by more than 30 points. The goal was in front of him, and it was not difficult to win. Suddenly, one shot missed the target, and Bolger scored 16 more points to finish. As a result, Bolger scored 600 points and Ding Mingyi scored 584 points. The high points are as follows: (Bolger) 30, 72, 35, 24, 20, 21, 30; (Ding Mingyi) 21, 21, 28, 46, 48, 28, 33, 24, 23, 28, 73.

Maxwell Wins with Steadiness

In the third game, Xu Shizhang and Maxwell of Britain were indeed strong opponents. Maxwell's final victory relied on his experience and steadiness. He was not reckless or negligent. His high points were only up to 40, but there were 11 scores over 20. Xu's skills were also superb, but his weakness was that he was too eager to try, often sacrificing a little point and giving the other party a good opportunity to advance. They approached each other several times, but it was difficult to maintain a difference within 100 points. Fortunately, in the last two shots, he scored 32 and 29 in a row. As a result, Xu scored 550 points and Maxwell scored 600 points. China lost another 50 points. The high points for the two are as follows: (Maxwell) 32, 23, 22, 123, 11, 40, 34, 34, 36, 31, 21; (Xu Shizhang) 20, Hole 5, 22, 22, 66, 32, 29.

Liangjiang Basketball Team's Southern Expedition (2): A 67-2 Victory Over the All-Star Team

(Manila Correspondence) The Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School basketball team showed its edge as soon as it arrived in the Philippines, defeating the All Nations Central School, a strong female team that dominates the Philippines, with a score of 49 to 13. The fierceness of their combat power and the excellence of their ball skills have left a deep impression on local Chinese and foreign people. On the afternoon of the 17th of last month at 4:30 PM, they went out for the second time and played against the All-Star team at the Saint Thomas basketball hall. Liangjiang showed great power and won a big victory over the All-Star team with a score of 67 to 2. The large difference in score has set a record that has never been seen in the Philippine women's basketball community. The following is a brief record of the battle:

Ms. Pan

Petite and Exquisite

It happened to be Sunday that day, so more than 2,000 people came to watch the game. The Shanghai team wore white shirts and green pants, and the Philippine team wore white shirts and black pants. At 4:30 PM, the two teams followed the referee Bao Dishi, and the whistle sounded. Liangjiang was very active from beginning to end, and the guards and forwards were brave and unparalleled. Before long, Chen Rongming received a ball from the back, stepped up a few steps, and scored the first goal. Not long after, Ms. Pan Meng and Ms. Chen Jucai successively scored points, and Ms. Pan was petite and exquisite, conquering east and west, and her footprints covered the entire field. The beauty of her shooting posture was praised by the audience. In the first quarter, Liangjiang took the lead with a score of 10 to 0.

Chen Rongming

Contributed Despite the Pain

The All-Star team, having suffered in the first quarter at the hands of Liangjiang, was eager to retaliate and used two people to monitor Dong Rongming and Chen Jucai. Not long after the second half began, Dong Rongming was injured in the head by the opponent's guard. Chen held his head and stopped the game. After a while, he continued the game despite the pain. Seeing him so brave, everyone applauded him. Liangjiang had Hu Zuo and Pan Meng enter the game. Before long, they scored points one after another. The two teams competed back and forth. The obese left forward of the All-Star team, Ms. Kiro, took the opportunity to foul Chen Baixue and got a free throw opportunity, making one of two attempts. The situation broke with a score of one to twenty, breaking the dull situation. At the end of the first half, Liangjiang was leading 24 to 1.

Philippine Miss

Indignant and Filled with Anger

After quenching their thirst, the two sides changed bases and fought again. Pan Meng showed her great skill in dodging, turning, and passing the ball, often working with Chen Rongming to attack. The score board high hung twenty-nine to one, and Liangjiang was still aggressive. The All-Stars could not resist. Chen Jucai and Pan Meng scored four more goals, making the score thirty-seven to one. At this time, Philippine Miss Annie took a risk and charged towards Liangjiang, attacking twice, but she was repelled by Chen Baixue and Bao Shuxia, and Liangjiang's defense was secure.

Hu Zuoqiong

Enters the Game Again

At the start of the fourth quarter, Hu Zuoqiong of Liangjiang entered the game to replace Pan Meng. The three wingers shot from left and right, and they were all successful. The score increased to sixty-three to one. Chen Rongming was injured in the head again by the opponent, but he continued to fight despite the pain. Later, the opponent scored one point from a free throw, making the score one to sixty-three. With one minute left in the game, Chen Rongming continued to be powerful, scoring two goals in a row. At the end of the game, Liangjiang played a triumphant song for the second time, winning 67 to 2.

Municipal Sports Field Organizes Basketball Association, Registration Starts on the 10th

The Municipal Sports Field Amateur Basketball Competition will be held once a year to hone the physique of citizens and promote basketball skills. It is reported that the fifth amateur basketball competition of this year will start registration on the 10th of this month and will end on the 31st. All amateur basketball teams from the business community are welcome to register. Each team is limited to 12 players. At the time of registration, a 6-inch photo of all team members must be attached (those who have not taken a full team photo can supplement it with individual photos), and their names and numbers must be marked on it for verification during the competition. The competition date is set for Saturday afternoon and Sunday all day, so that it does not interfere with the occupations of people from all walks of life. The competition will use a single round-robin system. If there are a large number of participating teams in the future, they will be divided into groups according to their ball skills, and each group will conduct a round-robin competition to increase the interest of the participants. Ministry of Education Supervises Middle Schools in Studying Education and Issues Outline for Research Associations

(Nanjing, 7th) The Ministry of Education has instructed all departments that in recent years, the ministry has successively formulated and promulgated standards for curricula and equipment in primary and secondary schools and normal schools, graduation examinations for students in middle and normal schools, and regulations for the certification of teachers in primary and secondary schools, in order to comprehensively improve and enhance educational efficiency. However, our country has a vast territory, and the circumstances of schools in various regions, due to historical legacy and geographical environment, are extremely different. The way to improve is to follow the central government's decrees on the one hand and to consider the actual situation in various localities and study implementation on the other, so as to promote benefits to the fullest extent and avoid the drawbacks of rigidity. Moreover, there are countless aspects of educational methods, and there are countless problems that need to be studied on the ground. Without research organizations, it is not easy to carry out reforms and obtain appropriate results. In order to supervise local schools in studying education issues, the ministry has specially formulated the "Outline of Measures for Provincial and Municipal Academic Teacher Training Education Research Associations" and the "Outline of Measures for Research on Guidance for Elementary Education", along with examples of research questions to be addressed, and issued them with an order. The ministry directs immediate establishment of research associations in accordance with the respective outlines to conduct research and to report the results of the research on the questions raised to the ministry for review by the end of May.

President Mei Yibao of Qilu University Declines Position

(Jinan, 7th) The future of Qilu University is not optimistic, as Mei Yibao has decided not to take the position of president of the university.

Madame Weydenthal, Wife of the Polish Envoy, Delivers a Celebrated Lecture at Jinling Women's University

At the invitation of the China-Poland Cultural Association and Jinling Women's Arts and Sciences College, Madame Weydenthal, wife of the Polish Envoy to China, accompanied Envoy Weydenthal to Nanjing on the 5th evening and gave a public lecture at Jinling Women's College. The topic was "The Contribution of Polish Women to the History and Culture of Their Country." Dr. Wu Yifang, President of Jinling Women's College, specially invited the Envoy and his wife to a tea party at the college at 4:00 p.m. on the 6th, accompanied by Ao Jingshi and Xie Shoukang, directors of the China-Poland Cultural Association, and others. Afterwards, she led Envoy Weydenthal and others on a tour of the college. Madame Weydenthal praised the college repeatedly. Foreign and Chinese people who came to listen to the lecture had already arrived successively. Among the foreign guests were Mr. and Mrs. Haas, Mr. and Mrs. Lee Hofer, Mr. and Mrs. Trier, Mr. Dantek, representatives of the League of Nations, members of various embassies and consulates, consultants and engineers from various countries, academic figures from various institutions in Nanjing, and students from various schools, totaling more than 500 people. Madame Weydenthal entered the auditorium, and President Wu delivered a speech, stating, "Madame Casimire Barthel de Weydenthal, the wife of Envoy Weydenthal, has been in China for a long time and has close ties with people in the academic community of our country. Madame Weydenthal is a scholar who has studied literature at the world-renowned Krakow University in Poland. Today, she has agreed to come to our college to lecture on the contribution of Polish women to the history and culture of their country, which will surely enable us to have a more precise understanding of Polish women, thereby promoting the rapprochement and understanding between our two nations. I am extremely happy and grateful," etc. Amidst applause, Madame Weydenthal stood up and lectured, giving a concise and clear account of important figures and general conditions of various eras of Polish women from the beginning of Polish history to the present. Her description of their participation in revolutionary work and their contribution to the revival of the Polish nation was particularly moving. The lecture ended at 6:40 p.m. In the evening at 8:00 p.m., Chu Minyi, Xie Shoukang, Chen Jianxiao, Guo Youshou, Ao Jingshi, directors of the China-Poland Association, hosted a banquet at the Association of Students Returning from Germany, Austria, and Switzerland. Honorary President Wu Zhihui, Chen Lifu, Zhang Daofan, Xu Beihong, Zhang Zhifu, and Dr. Wu Yifang and more than twenty others attended. They dispersed at past 10:00 p.m., having thoroughly enjoyed themselves. The translator for this event was Madame Zhang Wu Difeng, a professor at Central University. Madame Zhang had studied in France for many years, so her translation was very brilliant, and the entire audience praised it unreservedly.

Zhu Jiahao Offers Condolences on the Death of British Sinologist Giles

(Nanjing) Professor Giles, a British sinologist and professor at Cambridge University, passed away recently. The academic community in our country was deeply saddened upon hearing the news. Zhu Jiahao recently sent a telegram to his son, Dr. Lionel Giles, expressing his condolences.

Huang Yingbai and Li Jigu Support the Principles of the Ten Articles Declaration, Advocate Maintaining the Inherent Virtues of the Chinese Nation, Hope for Mutual Love Among Compatriots to Seek Self-Reliance, and Praise Famous Officials and Brave Generals as Models for People Today

Huang Yingbai's Opinion Huang Yingbai expressed his enthusiastic support for the Ten Articles Declaration with a very sincere attitude. Mr. Huang first stated that "The survival of a nation must have its conditions for survival. The most important principles we should promote today are self-reliance and harmonious coexistence among compatriots. To achieve self-reliance, we must first strive for the unity of the nation. To realize the unity of the nation, compatriots must first have the spirit of mutual love. This spirit is what the ancients called 'coming and going as friends, watching and helping each other, and supporting each other in sickness,' which is also the inherent virtue of our nation. If we do not preserve and promote it today, how can we talk about sincerely uniting to revitalize the nation? Mutual love among compatriots is an innate instinct. Since you all want to build a culture rooted in China, I hope you can inspire this spirit of mutual love among compatriots." He continued, "The Ten Articles Declaration will have a great impact on awakening the consciousness of young people. Currently, a portion of our country's youth often forgets their roots and clamors for world revolution, shouting long live for foreign countries. After this upheaval, they will surely realize that forgetting their roots is wrong." Finally, he solemnly stated, "Building a culture rooted in China is the responsibility of all Chinese people. Examining various countries in the world, whenever they are weak, there is always a 'nation-building' movement of this kind. I sincerely hope that this movement to build a culture rooted in China can be as powerful as the nation-building movements of other countries."

Li Jigu's Opinion Mr. Li Jigu, professor at Peking University and director of the Department of Literature and History at the Women's Arts and Sciences College, recently happened to be in Beijing. When discussing the Ten Articles Declaration, he said that he fully supports its principles, but the declaration has not yet mentioned specific plans. This aspect still needs to be considered and discussed by everyone. If a specific plan can be formulated so that all parties have something to follow, then the results may be even greater. He also said that in terms of material aspects, China is not truly poor. China simply cannot utilize all its wealth. If the Chinese people can develop their industries in a planned and down-to-earth manner, it may be possible to move from poverty to prosperity. Poverty is an inevitable disease. In terms of spiritual aspects, although China has always emphasized an ethical view of life, after the Song Dynasty, due to hypocrisy, many things were out of touch with human feelings, making it difficult for the people to know what to do or follow. In the last hundred years, due to the influence of Western civilization, the old morality has been discarded even more, and the morality of the new era has not yet been established or formed, causing the people to be even more bewildered. Intellectuals should pay close attention to this situation. He also said that from the standpoint of revitalizing the nation, the Ministry of Education should issue a unified order to promote famous officials and brave generals with integrity, such as Yue Wumu, Wen Tianxiang, and Fang Xiaoru, so that high officials and military generals have models to follow.

The Agricultural Studies Group of the Vocational Education Society National Investigation Team Departs Tomorrow First Stage Route Set to be Completed in Ten Months Investigation Targets Include Economy, Culture, and Politics

The National Rural Investigation Team organized by the Agricultural Studies Group of the Chinese Vocational Education Society, consisting of Xiang Shang, Yao Huizi, Wang Benren, Li Tao, and Zhong Tianshi, has been approved by the Ministry of Interior for the issuance of passports and is scheduled to depart tomorrow to begin the first stage of the journey, with a time limit of ten months. The route is as follows: Departing from Shanghai, passing through Xiamen, Hong Kong, and Guangzhou to Nanning as the first stop; proceeding from Nanning, passing through Baise, Nanlong, Xingyi, Chuping, and Qujing to Kunming as the second stop; proceeding from Kunming, passing through Xuanwei, Bijie, Naxi, Yibin, Jianwei, to Leshan, Mount Emei, Qingshen, Meizhou, Pengshan, Shuangliu, to Chengdu as the third stop. The investigation targets include: in terms of economy, agricultural products, animal husbandry, special products, and handicrafts; in terms of culture, education, religion, customs, and the status of women; in terms of politics, organization, security, transportation, and construction.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Fan Shushen)

Zhang the fortune teller said: "Next year, good fortune will shine brightly, and wealth and joy will come to your door." Li the fortune teller said: "A great disaster will surely occur within three days; going northwest will bring great luck." However, according to my thinking, if good fortune can be brought about and disaster can be avoided, then everyone born in the world must be blessed.

Some people say: If we use birds and beasts to compare human beings, then some are like majestic lions, some are like brave tigers and leopards, some are like cunning foxes, some are as poisonous as snakes and scorpions, some are as beautiful as peacocks, some are aware of current affairs like geese and swallows,... Some people say: If we use plants to compare human beings, then some people are like cold-resistant plums and bamboos, some are like evergreen pines and cypresses, some are like vines attached to other trees, some are like thorny roses,... However, various plants or animals can grow in the world, at least with some usefulness; however, what kind of animal or plant can those who only eat and do nothing be compared to!

Random Talk Among Couples, Old and Young

— Yi Sheng

The coordination of a couple is such that if their ages are similar, both will obtain "evenly matched" harmony in their physiology and daily life. However, driven by the power of love or other special relationships, it is also reasonable to expect that the age gap between the two sexes may be very different to form a match. In the past, there were many famous events in history that could serve as precedents, such as Duke Wen of Jin marrying Qi Jiang and Liu Xianzu marrying into the Eastern Wu. Among the common people, such things are even more like everyday meals, not worth being surprised at. Just like the marriage of a certain famous lawyer and a certain celebrity a few years ago, where the wife was older than the husband, it was said to be largely due to a mutual understanding; at that time, no one was discussing anything. This year, Xiong Xiling and Mao Yanwen's marriage, which matches an old man with a young wife, also belongs to people with status in society, but the matter came about by chance and has received great attention and criticism from society!

Recently, there was also an old Indian man, sixty years old, ten thousand miles away, who was about to marry a thirteen-year-old girl in a few days. That Indian saint, Gandhi, was greatly opposed to it and prepared to teach his followers to resist it. Three years ago, a similar event occurred, and Gandhi taught his disciples to form a funeral procession and accompany it along the road; this action has a bit of humorous meaning! If that marrying old man acted on his own initiative and preemptively, prepared a coffin to accompany him, and indicated that he wanted to fight to the death against his or her old age prospects, I'm afraid Gandhi would have no choice!

Gandhi is willing to incur resentment in order to safeguard humanitarianism: but he is too good at playing pranks and can be considered a saint of the times. From this point of view, it is better to be an old man, or an old Chinese man, to enjoy the advantage of being a new groom; to occupy the word "widower" among the four helpless poor people: widowers, widows, orphans, and the childless, in the past one was pitied by the royal government -- just according to Xiong's post-marital confession -- now no one will actually carry out sabotage.

Anecdotes About Cigarette Packets

— Zheng Yimei

Cigarettes have been in our country for decades. My friend Qian Huafo does not smoke, but he likes to collect cigarette cases and packets, collecting everything, which is a grand sight. He glues them into albums, a number of volumes, and he is ingenious in his organization. For example, he combines the World brand with the Peace brand to form World Peace, and the Central brand with the Committee brand to form Central Committee. He also combines the Sun Yat-sen, Zijin Mountain, Longevity Mountain, Ma Zhanshan, and Wanbaoshan five brands into the Five Mountains Chart. He also demonstrates clever thinking. Also, the White Phoenix brand box shows a chicken, and the Dog brand shows a dog's head. When asked, he says: "This is a chicken crowing and a dog stealing." On another page, he glues a certain cigarette box from Japan, below which are the Bandit brand and the Great Wall brand, saying: "This also has a slight meaning, but the meaning is quite obvious and not difficult to guess." The most auspicious combination is to combine the Golden Brand, Ruyi Brand, Long Happiness Brand, and Great Harvest Brand into one page. Seeing it makes people happy. This is truly a good song and prayer. Others, such as the Pinhai brand, are marked as produced in the 25th year of Guangxu, with a price of sixteen texts per box; the Bicycle brand, produced in the 32nd year of Guangxu, with a price of eighteen texts per box; the Rickshaw brand, produced in the third year of Xuantong, is marked as the rickshaw brand commonly known, with five sticks per pack, sold for five texts. Seeing this is enough to see the huge difference in prices between today and the past. Also, the Phoenix Call brand, with a colorful phoenix painted on the box, is said to be produced by Hongwu Tobacco Company in the second year of the Republic of China, founded by Bai Liewu. It has now disappeared from the market. Huafo further pointed to the White Gold Dragon brand and said: "This is the cigarette that Zhang Taiyan liked to smoke." Old Knife brand said: "This is the cigarette that Tianxu Wosheng liked to smoke." Beauty brand said: "This is what Zheng Mantuo and Li Jinhui both loved to smoke." Others, such as the relationship between art performers and the Pyramids, and the relationship between laborers and the Golden Mouse brand, all seem to have a close and inextricable connection. Therefore, the taste of smoking can reveal the person's position and character. Huafo is a thoughtful person with insightful observations. I am writing this anecdote to record it.

Petty Theft

— Zhu Ying

This time, Mr. Zhang's family in our alley caught a petty thief. This petty thief, around 5:30 in the afternoon, when dusk was approaching, slipped into Mr. Zhang's half-open front door and stole a summer wool jacket and a lined overcoat. He was just about to sneak away when Mr. Zhang caught him and grabbed him.

The cry of "Mr. Zhang's family caught a petty thief" immediately spread throughout the alley. The noise was so loud, everyone rushed to Mr. Zhang's door to see the excitement. Driven by curiosity, I also squeezed in to see what was going on. When I got to Mr. Zhang's door, I saw the petty thief kneeling in front of Mr. Zhang, kowtowing repeatedly.

Mr. Zhang saw me, nodded and greeted me, so I squeezed forward and glanced at the petty thief kneeling on the ground, and couldn't help but be startled, because the petty thief was actually Yu Guisheng, who had been my next-door neighbor three years ago. So I couldn't help but blurt out, "Yu Guisheng, how did you get into this kind of thing?" The petty thief paused when he heard me call his name, then recognized me and said with tears streaming down his face, "Sir, alas, ever since the factory closed down, for the past four years, I haven't been able to find work. My old mother, wife, and children have all been starving for three or four years. We've eaten everything and pawned everything we have, and I couldn't think of any other way, so I started doing this. I've done it three times, and never been caught. Today I was caught. I beg you, sir, please be lenient. If I'm sent to the authorities, my whole family will starve to death." I felt somewhat sympathetic after hearing this. Mr. Zhang saw that I knew him, so he didn't want to send him to the police. Yu Guisheng quickly crawled on the ground and kowtowed to me and Mr. Zhang. Then, a thin, gaunt figure disappeared into the dark entrance of the alley.

When I got home, I felt my eyes were a little wet.

Shared Suffering

Records of Lingering Fragrance

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of Qing, translated by Qin Shouou

Peeking down from the gap in the sedan curtain, I could only see the yellow sand on the ground quickly receding behind us, which showed how fast our sedan was traveling. It made me recall how high our spirits were when we left the palace and went to the train station on this same sandy road just over ten days ago? It felt like only yesterday! Before long, we had entered the Imperial City, and the city gates were wide open on both sides, welcoming us in without any hesitation.

However, this was not the final destination of our journey! The Empress Dowager would definitely not stay here. Although this was indeed the center of the Imperial City, the depths of the inner court, the so-called central hub; the Empress Dowager had never liked this place!

"How old and dilapidated this place is!" She once clearly expressed her dissatisfaction with this palace. She said, "Besides the many tall and inappropriate buildings, it's simply empty and devoid of anything! As soon as we make the slightest sound, it will evoke a huge echo; making us feel terrified. Even that Imperial Garden has no decorations; it's full of tall, gloomy old trees, with no bright flowers or gentle breeze. This place is simply filled with a cold, lifeless atmosphere, without the slightest hint of vitality!"

Because of this reason, she spent more than seven-tenths of her later life in the Summer Palace. However, today we have just returned from Fengtian, and logically speaking, we must first come to the palace: if there were no such customary restrictions, she would have gone directly to the Summer Palace after leaving the train station. Small Recipes

Home Cooking

— Zhu Yun

Preserving Vegetables: In spring, when the apricot trees are in bloom, the rapeseed flowers in the fields are a vibrant yellow, very eye-catching. This type of rapeseed, when it is just sprouting and hasn't yet flowered, is called "vegetable heart"; it is a common spring vegetable, and is very delicious when boiled as a vegetarian dish. When this "vegetable heart" is tender, wash it clean, then boil it in a pot with water, take it out and dry it on bamboo poles or ropes in the sun. This dried "vegetable heart" is called "dried vegetable head," and it can be stored for a long time without spoiling in a dry earthenware jar or pot. When cooking this "dried vegetable head," it must first be soaked in boiling water until it is plump, and then you can start cooking. Spinach and horsehair also can be boiled, dried, and stored for later use, and they have a cool, unique flavor when eaten.

Bamboo Shoots and Sweet Bamboo Shoots: In the spring, bamboo shoots are certainly the only famous vegetable. The taste of bamboo shoots is fresh and delicious, and whether boiled or used in vegetarian dishes, they are always fresh, refreshing, and flavorful. However, bamboo shoots are seasonal, and while they are tender in February and March, as spring fades, the bamboo shoots also sprout leaves and become new bamboo, at which point they become old and inedible. Therefore, in addition to canned goods, Suzhou families also have several ways to preserve bamboo shoots. There are usually two common methods. First, cut the bamboo shoots into thin strips, and boil them with soy sauce, etc., then take them out and dry them in the sun. Another method is to also cut the bamboo shoots into thin strips, and boil them with soy sauce and sugar together, then dry them slightly in the sun and store them for later use. These sweet bamboo shoots are all made from tender bamboo shoots and are exceptionally delicious.

Cured Meat and Dried Fish: Fresh fish, meat, and vegetables are certainly fresh, delicious, and fatty, but pickled and cured foods also have a unique flavor. At the end of the year and the beginning of the new year, after washing the fresh fish or meat, first marinate it with salt, then soak it in soy sauce for one or two weeks to allow the salty taste of the soy sauce to penetrate into the fish or meat, then take it out and dry it in the sun, and hang it under the eaves in a ventilated place, where it can be stored for a long time without spoiling. Because this fish or meat has been soaked in soy sauce, the fat is not greasy, and the lean meat is even more bright red, almost like ham. Cured meat is most popular when spring bamboo shoots come on the market, and cooking it with fresh meat is the most seasonal home-style dish during the Qingming Festival. Dried fish, stewed with wine, is so refreshing and delicious that it is truly not inferior to southern ham!

Pea Shoots, Lettuce, and Water Shield: Pea shoots are the vines of peas. Suzhou people call them "pea vines," and stir-frying them with shrimp meat has a wonderful synergistic effect. In recent years, they have been canned for storage, so they are available in all seasons. Lettuce is refreshing and delicious when eaten fresh, and Suzhou wild game shops and candy stores make lettuce into sliced shoots, which are green and very pleasing to the eye. As for water shield, it is also a special product of Taihu Lake, and it is exceptionally delicious when cooked with shredded chicken during the Qingming period. However, the flavor of canned water shield is far inferior to the fresh version.

Small Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 10: Rudely Displaying Wealth Before a Young Woman, Coveting the Wall and Getting Sick, Losing Integrity

So he continued, I'm just relaying what Master Jia said. Whether you agree or not is naturally up to you two women. I can't force you, can I? If you're saying your family is waiting for the money to live on, there's money to take back right away, what's wrong with that? It's good that you've already agreed to give yourself to Master Jia, it's not like a random stranger. If you agree now, according to you, you'd pick a date, and after picking a good date, wouldn't you still have to send the girl to this hotel to accompany him? Sooner rather than later, I don't think there's anything wrong with that. As he said this, he smiled obsequiously at the others. What did Zhu Hush know? After listening to what the matchmaker said, she thought it over and over and felt that what he said made sense. Since she had agreed to give the girl to him, what did it matter if she gave her sooner rather than later? As long as she could take this pile of silver dollars home, she could take care of so many things. If the girl stayed here, it wasn't like he'd take a piece of her flesh, at most it would just be like she'd become a bride in a daze. As she thought this in her heart, she couldn't help but steal a few glances at the pile of silver dollars, then looked at the girl again. She thought to herself, thinking that people are about to starve to death, what's the point of talking about face? Like selling the girl a few years ago and sending her to someone else? So she said to the matchmaker, Mr. Zhang, am I just leaving her here like this? Although she was brave enough to ask this question, she was still timid, and her voice trembled as she spoke, and the words were also vague. (151)

The US Dollar No Longer Devalues: New York Stock Market Plunges After Rising

According to a report from the New Feng Foreign Firm, yesterday (the 6th), the New York stock market fell to a new low. A counselor from the White House solemnly declared that President Roosevelt's remarks at a press conference did not in any way imply a further reduction in the gold content of the US dollar. After talking with reporters in the morning, Wall Street speculators believed that Roosevelt's words hinted at the possibility of another devaluation of the dollar. Mining stocks rose sharply, and other stocks followed suit. The rise was further fueled by short covering and the weakness of the dollar. At the same time, grains also soared, and government bonds plummeted, causing anxiety to the Treasury Department, which was about to issue new bonds. Roosevelt then instructed his counselor to explain his remarks, stating that all speculation about a further devaluation of the dollar was entirely unfounded. After this statement was released, market trends immediately reversed, with stocks plunging, government bonds rebounding, the dollar strengthening, and grains falling. In the afternoon session, the current month became firmer due to brisk trading by out-of-town merchants, while distant months remained weak due to the continued decline in gold prices. However, trading volume was light as both buyers and sellers were hesitant. As a result, the current month fell by 0.075 yuan, April fell by 0.0175 yuan, May fell by 0.02 yuan, June fell by 0.03 yuan, July fell by 0.0275 yuan, and August fell by 0.0225 yuan.

Transactions in all months of the wheat market were sluggish. Prices were based on imported wheat, and the decline in gold prices naturally softened sentiment. However, although the wheat market is related to foreign exchange rates, buyers must have physical goods to engage in legitimate trading, which is different from pure speculation. Therefore, selling pressure was light in both the morning and afternoon, resulting in only a weak market and limited declines. As a result, March and April each fell by 0.03 yuan, and August fell by 0.03 yuan. The spot wheat market saw firm prices for high-quality wheat, while medium and lower-quality wheat were average. Shandong Dezhou and Suzhou wheat opened at 3.77 yuan, and Bengbu Mingguang, Xinpu, and Fuzhou wheat opened at 3.75 yuan. Neixin sold 2,500 bags, and Shenda sold 1,000 bags.

Zhongguan Thin Rice Recovers Slightly

Dujian, Yinbianyuan, and other varieties also showed no fluctuations.

Market prices saw white japonica recover by 0.1 to 0.2 yuan, and thin rice tightened by a few fen. The prices of other goods were similar to before.

Yesterday's selling prices were similar to the previous day, but the situation was very good. If sales continue to be strong in the future, there may be hope for further price increases. Hunan Jihong rice (customer xiān) was purchased by traders here for domestic use at 250 bags, with a price of 10.023 yuan, an increase of 0.1 yuan compared to the previous market.

Yesterday, the soybean market maintained the good market conditions of the previous day, but it was difficult for the overall trend to rise because purchasing power was weak and prices stopped rising when they reached a certain level. The association's clearing price for No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was raised by 0.1 yuan to 17 yuan, but there was no demand. Re-export goods were priced at 4.95 yuan, with 250 bags traded. Zhenyu No. 1 was priced at 16.5 yuan, No. 2 at 16.4 yuan, No. 3 at 16.25 yuan, and No. 4 at 16.1 yuan. Dried and Preserved Goods: Shima Longan Arrives in Small Quantities

Shima longan was said to have been difficult to negotiate due to the influx of Quanzhou inferior goods last winter, resulting in very favorable prices. As inventory of small and medium-sized grains of general shipments dwindled, prices gradually improved, and Shima longan is also approaching a suitable price. It was found that some goods have already arrived through Guangzhou轮轮, and the market is expected to open in a few days.

Oil Market: Hongjiang Tung Oil's Rising Trend Has Subsided

Since the spring trading of Hongjiang tung oil in this port, the price of secondary Hongjiang oil has been stable at 23.4 yuan per barrel. Until last week, the new first trading price in Zhenjiang was also publicly negotiated and opened, and the calculated price was similar to the spring trading price negotiated in this port. However, after trading, it seemed that it was smart, and it is now heard that the numbers have not been fixed, and the market has become nervous. Last night, a telegram came from Zhenjiang saying that Zhenghong, Jichang, and He tung oil must be sold for 28 yuan per barrel, and secondary Hongjiang oil will not be sold. Although it was not explicitly stated how much it would increase, the implication was obvious, and it was expected that it would increase by 0.7 or 0.8 yuan. The reason for the increase is nothing more than the influence of white tung oil. Since white tung oil has soared, the cost of Hongjiang tung oil has also increased, and the production volume of each oil pressing workshop may have decreased as a result. Therefore, the new goods currently arriving may be hoarded for profit. The lowest limit for the selling price of secondary Hongjiang oil in this port is expected to be around 24 yuan.

Free Talk

"A Dog Bites Lü Dongbin"

— Hanfeng

Zheng of Changle edited and printed "Miscellaneous Dramas of the Qing Dynasty," which includes four kinds of dramas by Ye Chengzong (Yi Sheng). The "Kong Fang Brother" excerpt "is a dramatized theory of the god of money, which expresses the greatness of the power of the god of money through the solo of the Confucian scholar Jin Geng, and is a work of anger at the world" (Xi Di's interpretation). The power of the so-called god of money can move ghosts and gods, so Jin Geng sang:

Heaven also loves money, the Heavenly Money Star shines in the blue sky;

The earth also loves money, the ancient Qiantang surges with the Zhejiang tide;

The wood also loves money, the elm money drifts in the spring painting;

The flowers also love money, the golden money flowers are beautiful;

The horse also loves money, the golden money horse has a high price;

The leopard also loves money, the golden money leopard roars with its nature;

The gods also love money, they ask about the six lines with golden money;

Ghosts also love money, they burn paper money on the road to the underworld;

The literati also love money, they select young talents with green money;

The warriors also love money, they compete with golden money in archery.

This song "Rear Courtyard Flower" explains that money is loved by everyone, loved by animals, and loved by ghosts and gods. "What will happen if there is no money for a day?" This is the fact, so Ye Chengzong satirically concludes: "Father Kong Fang, I only rely on your knees, I beg you, Chunting," and says that if there is no money for a day, then:

The pot is short of grain, the stove is short of firewood, the kitchen is short of fine food, the jar is short of fragrant wine;

Friends are few, relatives are few, wives are nagging, servants are chattering;

There is skin but no hair, there is meat but no fat, the belly is empty, the foolish dream is in vain;

The heart is like oiled, the throat is like smoked, the sweat is like pouring, the eyes are like shaking bells;

It is difficult to escape with wings, it is difficult to be spared, it is difficult to eliminate the suffering, it is difficult to endure the living sin;

There is no exchange for borrowing, there is no pride for beggars, there is no nest for selling, there is no robe for pawning;

Try hard to frown and cannot get half a cent, only to end up dry and anxious! (Qing Ge Er!)

Ye Chengzong's indignation can be imagined here. However, what he hates seems not to be "money" itself, but the "dogs" who run errands for officials. He wrote the four-act "A Dog Bites Lü Dongbin," and his purpose was probably here, although he ultimately could not avoid fantasy, wanting to awaken the "dogs" so that they could also become immortals, recover their spirituality, and ascend to immortality together.

The story, as Xi Di said, "uses the common saying 'a dog bites Lü Dongbin, not knowing a good person' as a point, and Pingdu adds Shi Jie as a person, with the matter of Dongbin leading Jie to become an immortal as the center. "The wedge says that Dongbin travels around and passes by Mount Tai. He sees the scholar Shi Youdao in the clouds and decides to save him. The first act says that Dongbin acts as a wandering monk to enlighten Shi Jie, asking him to donate to build a temple, but Jie at this time is:

All the scraping in the house is nothing more than incomplete notes;

All the investigation in the belly cannot help your front and back mansion;

All the flapping in the mouth cannot be worth a rafter or tile. (That Zha Ling)

He doesn't even have a place to insert this five-zang temple. Finally, Dongbin asks for "a clear conversation for one night, which is also a predestined relationship." He feels that Shi Jie is a person who "still has the habits of a celebrity, and this is the root of the disaster." The second act writes that Lü Jie returns to the city to visit friends the next day, and meets Cai Qi, a night patrol officer, and his dog, which is "quite capable of biting people." Lü Jie is used to "wearing casual clothes and having a mountain forest nature," and does not pay attention to it, so he is taken down. He hates it extremely, scolding Cai Qi:

I have heard of your name for a long time, and only now do I know Jing. It is nothing more than cats and mice in the public hall, fire consumption and levies, fines and punishments. I ask you, brother, do you have Cai Jing? Besides this, what virtue do you have? What face do you have to compete with people? (Shang Xiao Lou)

Cai Qi "can't beat him, can't talk him down," and tells the dog to bite him and send him to the east corridor of the Tai Temple to freeze, preparing to freeze him to death. But Shi Jie is not afraid, nor does he submit. He continues to scold all the way, scolding all the way to the Tai Temple:

Could it be that the Old Mother of Mount Tai has no divinity, and allows this living being under her feet? You wield authority and issue orders, you set fire and I will not allow you to light lanterns. (Yao Hai Er)

The third act writes that Dongbin learns of this matter and goes to enlighten him again. He first instructs the Willow Tree Spirit: "Shi Sheng is trapped, and I want to enlighten Cai Qi. I am afraid that he will not understand, so only at noon, create wind and fog, and the sky will be dark. Cai Qi will surely be afraid, and Shi Sheng will be released." Then he goes to find Cai Qi himself, but unexpectedly, the dog suddenly comes out and bites Dongbin, biting him many times. Dongbin then bursts out scolding the dog:

Ah! I only see a fierce dog coming out of the vermilion door, showing the power of the eastern people. Dog, the lanugo on your head has not yet receded, and you are already showing off your power... (Xiao Tao Hong)

Dog! Waiting to eat, you have things, you can't say whether the warehouse has surplus grain or is hungry. There are so many vagrants in the ditch, but you, the killer, eat your fill and have no scruples... (Tiao Xiao Ling)

You make me furious with your wolf's heart and dog's lungs, and deceive good people since ancient times. Even if you are a divine mastiff, you will be killed by Mi Ming. What dog knowledge, what dog scheming, what infatuation! (Tu Si Er) Dogs rely on people's power, like tigers helping foxes. Laughing at vicious dogs barking and disturbing Yao, it is your dog party that is doing this. (Ma Lang Er)

Then Dongbin casts a spell to threaten Cai Qi and release Lü Jie. But at this time, the dog also changed its appearance. "Looking at this dog, I only see it begging for pity and wagging its tail. Could it be that the dog also intends to turn its heart back?" The fourth act is probably a long time later. Lü Jie "passed the imperial examination and was appointed censor. He returned to his hometown in brocade," and he felt that "prosperity and decline are things that people cannot know, as if they were in the Road of Handan." But Cai Qi was distressed, fearing that he would take revenge, so he hurriedly repaired Shi Jie's old residence to atone for his previous sins. Shi Jie found it ridiculous and instead rebuked him, "Who told you to repair my Shi's old thatched cottage where books are stored? How dare you chop down the plum blossoms in front of my small window!" When he saw the dog begging for pity and wagging its tail, he sang again:

Yesterday you were dancing your claws and baring your teeth, wagging your head and tail, and biting each other fiercely, showing off your rudeness. How can you now wag your tail and beg for pity, hang your head and lose your temper, with all kinds of tones? Don't expect me to spare you lightly. (Tian Shui Ling)

At this time, Dongbin comes again to save Shi Jie, and Jie also feels that this time of being an official is "forced into a monkey suit, learning to be a puppet, only to end up with his tail bare," so he "takes off his court clothes, puts on a cloth robe, removes his precious belt, ties a silk cord, puts on straw shoes and throws away his boots, changes his nine-sun scarf, and dresses up as an immortal" (Gu Mei Jiu), "never entering the circle of fame and fortune again," and the "dog" is also saved along with him.

The general situation of the whole drama is like this. It is easy to understand that the author, Ye Chengzong, is a person with a belly full of complaints. In "Kong Fang Brother," he curses money; in "Thirteen Niang," he laments "Hearing about injustice makes his eyes split, who can borrow the chivalrous heart?"; in "Jia Langxian," he indignantly points out that writing is useless, "but empty fame and noise cannot save him from the cold." And "Lü Dongbin" is even more indignant and scolds fiercely, from Cai Qi to the Celestial Mastiff.

He used articles to criticize the social injustice and political corruption of the time, hoping that great immortals and chivalrous people would come out. It is not surprising that a writer who grew up in a feudal society would have such views. However, his expectations seem to be more than that, that is, he not only hopes that these "injustices in the world" will be eliminated by the immortals and heroes, but also hopes that those bandit-like people can also be saved and lay down their butcher knives.

This is the consistent thought of Taoism, and it is also the consistent unrealistic fantasy. At that time, Ye Chengzong was not the only writer who was like this.

One Day

— Qian Dong

I woke up early in the morning, holding a pen and rustling, preparing to write something I could be satisfied with. However, my mother was also scraping the remaining rice in the rice box with a rustling sound.

The rice is gone again!

I put down my pen; I couldn't write anything more.

My mother was quietly counting the days, the seventh, the eighth… She took the remaining rice downstairs to wash it, muttering to herself, "Why are we eating so fast?"

My wife, who was washing diapers, rushed upstairs in a hurry. She whispered to me anxiously, "We have to buy rice again today. Go out in the afternoon!"

I nodded. She ran back downstairs to wash diapers.

My younger sister smiled, tidied her books, and went to school.

The sun had already touched the ground. I wanted to pick up my pen again, but the child sleeping in the cradle started coughing fiercely again. He cried so pitifully, like a lone ape wailing under the pale moonlight, lingering and mournful. This had been going on for four days.

I put down my pen again, dragged the cradle over, and sang a lullaby to him with my withered voice. But he still cried so mournfully, his two tearful little eyes fixed on me, crying to me with "咿咿嗚嗚," and I didn't understand his words.

At this moment, this sound was so sad that I simply couldn't listen. I once thought that if I killed him with a knife, he wouldn't resist at all. Perhaps when the blade touched his neck, he would think I was treating his cough-broken throat. It was because of this defenseless blade that I gently retracted the sword that had killed many powerful enemies. Instead, this defenseless blade pierced my heart!

In the past, I always felt that men should never cry, no matter what. Now, I was crying at the child's withered face, and tears streamed down profusely.

Lunch was already cooked, and my younger sister was home from school, but we didn't have the usual joyful sounds.

My mother silently ate a shallow bowl of rice and stopped.

"What? There's still rice," I said.

"No, I'm very full. When I woke up this morning, my stomach felt a bit full, stuffy," she said, hiccupping.

My wife only ate one bowl of rice and stopped, saying she felt a bit unwell. My younger sister also put down her rice bowl. I uneasily ate one bowl of rice and also put down my chopsticks.

The child started crying again. My wife, holding the child, stared at me and said, "Then, are you going out in the afternoon?"

"Yes, I'll go out!"

I replied. I brushed the dust off my clothes, wiped my worn-out leather shoes, and left.

The sky became overcast, and a brown wind blew wildly. The roads were like a dense spider web, one here, one there. Streetcars and cars flew back and forth in the brown wind. I hesitated, asking myself:

"Where to go?"

Dead Emotions

— Wei Zhongtian

It's still a night with such a clear moon, still a small path with willows planted on both sides, just like three years ago, when I walked through with my lonely and isolated heart, I would stand still, or wander around, raising my head to look at the sparkling stars, lowering my head to look at my shadow, making all kinds of absurd dreams, and in the end, when I got tired, I would leave the small path with a dry laugh. But now I still walk through such a small path alone, however, this situation can no longer inspire me to make those absurd dreams, and all the sentimental emotions of the past are dead.

So-called "youth," so-called "happiness," have deceived me of a lot of enthusiasm, a lot of tears, and made me spend a lot of long years in boredom. Now I have awakened, and from now on I will no longer be absurd or stupid, and I will no longer bite my fingers in sorrow and disappointment.

Young people should have vigor and a strong will. The difficult life of the past few years has told me that it is not okay for a person to be too weak. Being disheartened and negative by any small stimulus or slight blow is not what a young person should be. Such a young person will eventually be abandoned on the beaches on both sides of the rolling tide. It is not bad for a person to encounter various difficulties and harsh environments when they are young, because in this environment, a person is often tempered to be stronger and more capable. I myself was rescued from a harsh environment and learned a lot of life knowledge. Today, I have even more courage to deal with the difficulties of the future.

Even though I say that, I still feel that my recent days have been a bit stupid, which may be because my desires are too great and too deep, so I feel dissatisfied and stupid in any environment! I have a lot of hopes. If hope turns into disappointment, it is of course bitter. Fortunately, if hope really reaches its goal, I will feel the boredom of being ordinary and boring. This often makes me feel that life is terribly stupid! Who can I blame for this? I can only blame myself. There was a time when I always hoped to come to Japan to see the autumn leaves, thinking that sitting under the maple trees, reading my favorite books, and picking one or two leaves when I was happy to put in my favorite books as bookmarks, and after one or ten years, when I had the opportunity to reopen that favorite book, and found the maple leaves, recalling all the situations at that time, would be very pleasant. Now, I have seen the maple leaves, but what do the maple leaves give me? Nothing. If I have to say, it is that pile of melancholy.

The weather is getting warmer day by day, and there seems to be a little bit of spring in the sunlight. Soon, spring will come again. Wait, when spring comes, the cherry blossoms will also bloom. Cherry blossoms, the two words "cherry blossoms" have also made me love them. I dare not say anything now. After seeing the cherry blossoms, I will record my mood.

Recently, I seem to feel a little lonely, so the day before yesterday I bought a purple vase and a bunch of purple flowers (I like purple the most) and put them on my desk, thinking to adjust this life. When I am tired, I will smell these flowers, and I am full of thinking that there is a lot of warmth in the breath of these flowers to convey to me, but, disappointingly, they only give me a stuffy feeling of irritability, yes, this should be the case, because all those emotions of the past are dead.

Toward Evening (16)

— Qu Yi

"Oh! It turned out to be such a big bedbug!"

"A bedbug?" The new literary man sitting in the bathroom heard the discussion about bedbugs next door, and suddenly had an inspiration. He thought, "When I was in Japan, bedbugs were called Nanjing bugs. But now, when the national economy is bankrupt, we scholars have all become bedbug class."

However, Hu Yiyuan, sitting on the bed, shook his hand to stop the red-headed literary man from making fun of the female bedbug.

"In short, even though it's a bedbug, it's stinging in your heart! In your heart—"

"Haha!" There was a burst of laughter full of vitality. But in the laughter, there was suddenly a strange voice mixed in: "Young master! Young master!"

It wasn't until the laughter stopped that there was a voice, "You dump it out and take a look." – It was a voice with a bit of terror.

Hu Yiyuan immediately dragged his slippers out, but he couldn't find the broadcaster of the familiar voice in the room. The two "female army commanders" sitting beside the drunkard, stroking, caressing, laughing, and hugging, each indulging in the teasing of men and women, pointed their mouths at Hu Yiyuan towards the door, signaling. Hu Yiyuan went out the door again. Just a second. Hu Yiyuan came in with a panicked expression. The light in the room immediately turned pale.

"Go! Go! You get out of here quickly! The goods are here! The goods!"

As soon as they heard the word "goods," they, who originally belonged to the bedbug class, were naturally startled. Although they were smiling, their hearts had never been at ease for a moment. This was their life in the evening. Hu Yiyuan's somewhat surprised "go, go" sound, like the wind blowing through the cracks in the wall, naturally had a quick reaction at the end of their nerves. They immediately quietly retreated with solemn expressions. Then, Hu Yiyuan asked the red-headed literary man and Li An, who was still drunk and walking across half the country, to leave. Then he pulled his uncle again and whispered in his uncle's ear:

"It's over! Uncle, the trick has been exposed. That lottery ticket! That flood prize! Oh! Hurry! Let's go first. It's better to leave first!…"

The two of them also staggered out.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Comments

The Worst Year for Youth

— Chen

As the calendar for 1934 is placed on our desks, many political commentators and forecasters are crying out about the economic panic and the crisis of war, until the day of the "Great World Breakdown."

Mr. Di'aike, the secretary-general of the New York Christian Youth Association, said in his work report for 1934 that this year was one of the worst years for youth in American history. "The tragedy and heinousness of their panorama can hardly be determined forever, because the decline of spiritual and moral qualities is subtle and invisible, and difficult to statistically analyse. However, the wreckage of humanity is shocking, which is a fact. This moral decline is the result of the youth era spent in a world of war, followed by world reconstruction, unhealthy prosperity, and recession." It is also said that they feel "not needed by the world".

General idealists always explain the "moral decline" of mankind as caused by spiritual inferiority or lack of education, while neglecting the economic and material reasons. However, we will never doubt that the Anglo-Saxon youth, who have always prided themselves on being civilized, are spiritually inferior or lack education, but they "spent their youth in a world of war" and loved "the unhealthy prosperity and recession" causing them not to be needed by the noble, and therefore "morality declined". Just as we have unemployed college students, we produce "higher-level hooligans" who open schools to collect money, and the fact of college students stealing.

However, what we want to say is that the "moral decline" of youth comes with the end of the world and the current society. It is true that youth are "irresponsible," as Mr. Di'aike said, but it cannot be "remedied" by the "spiritual cultivation" used by organizations such as the New York Youth Association. Obviously, the center of current spiritual corruption is not in the general youth, but in the society that creates "unhealthy prosperity and recession" and the rule of this part of the people. It is precisely because of its existence that youth are in "a world of war," "not needed by the world," which leads to moral decline. Holding the doctrine of "spiritual cultivation" cannot break this environment, nor make him needed by the world, nor can he easily "follow up with world reconstruction."

We should not forget that it is always those "morally declining" slaves who can rebuild the world.

Little Fifth Uncle

— Jiang Tian

Fifth Uncle's age has passed his fifties, but because of his usual talkativeness and laughter, he doesn't look like an old man. So the children don't call him Fifth Uncle, but add a small character to the words Fifth Uncle, and everyone calls him Little Fifth Uncle. He doesn't get angry when he hears the children calling him that, but instead, he plays with the children as if he is happy.

Little Fifth Uncle can be regarded as a monster. He has liked to play since he was a child, and he hasn't changed his nature even when he is old. According to him, he has been running around the north and south since he was a child, and he has traveled to most of the major cities and small villages in many provinces. He knows all kinds of people, but he has never had trouble with anyone, and everyone can call him brother.

Having this kind of skill is not bad. But one thing is that he was born poor from his mother's womb, and he is still poor after half a century. He was a soldier during the Qing Dynasty, participated in the revolution during the revolution, worked as a waiter, worked as a long-term worker, worker, farmer, and did all kinds of chores. He has also been to Southeast Asia, so he often

Page 19

He often says to people: all the secrets of the world have been done, and he has tasted a lot of flavors. When he was forty years old, he settled down in his hometown to farm. He also found a wife for his son. But after a few years, his wife died, and he didn't have any problems, he was still as happy as a child, as if he didn't have any worries. When he was fifty years old, although his daughter-in-law had given birth to several children, none of them survived, and his son, who was in good health in his early twenties, died this year. This made him disappointed in everything, and the old man had to watch a young daughter-in-law live alone. Although he was unhappy in his heart, his old tune of talking and laughing was still as good as ever.

The children all liked him. When I was a child, I would ask him to tell jokes as soon as I saw him, as if he told them better than others.

As I grew older, I didn't have much contact with Little Fifth Uncle, but I couldn't forget his shadow in my mind. I was only seventeen when his son died. From that year on, I left my hometown and didn't go home. It wasn't until one lunar New Year three years ago that I returned to my hometown, which I hadn't seen for several years.

Walking into the gate of my hometown, I thought of Little Fifth Uncle. Little Fifth Uncle used to come to my house often. He knew I was back and would definitely come to see me, but after waiting for a day, I didn't see his shadow come to my house. The next morning, after getting out of bed, I asked my mother, and my mother said:

"He's already dead. He died last year. I forgot to tell you."

My mother said as she walked down the stairs. At this time, I was stunned when I heard my mother's words, and I was always thinking: would Little Fifth Uncle, who was lively and like a child, die so quickly? What about his young widow? I was thinking in my heart, and my feet couldn't help but move, and I ran towards his house.

Turning around and walking through a few quiet paths, I arrived at the entrance of Little Fifth Uncle's house. I looked at the door panel, the stone steps, the copper door ring, and the two faded good fortune characters on the door panel. Everything was like the old courtyard. Only the two white paper and black characters couplets were newly pasted on the door panel. I gently knocked on the door ring a few times, and the two wooden doors opened with a creak.

"Oh! Is it Uncle Zhi? Please come in and sit down!"

A middle-aged woman flashed before my eyes. She said something and let me go in first. As I walked, I said:

"Sister-in-law is still living here, is everything okay? Why don't you come to our house to play? You have to be happy during the New Year!"

She walked behind me, but didn't say a word. I sat and talked in the hall where Fifth Uncle's spiritual tablet was enshrined for a while and then left.

"There's no fun in living alone. People like Little Fifth Uncle have never had a good life until they get old. After they die, they leave a widow. She's only twenty-four or five years old this year, which is the period of youth. Has she endured it for a few years, and does she still want to endure it? In today's world, it's not easy to keep chastity. Let's be a nun. In this era, being a nun is not necessarily completely pure. What else does she want?"

As I thought, I walked, and I had already arrived at the entrance of my house.

Glorious Days

— Hua Zhi

It was the second spring since Genbao was released from prison.

Except for the winter when his father built three new thatched huts, he had spent a smiling New Year with flowered paper money. After that, he only spent a series of difficult New Years in sighs and sighs. Although in memory, drinking, gambling, singing community dramas, and secretly meeting with Sister Zhao behind the mountain, the deprivation of this kind of beautiful dream felt difficult. But every day, when he got up from the bed, he had to find a way to make two meals of rice porridge for the family. It was difficult to bear the hunger, and even if he thought of the grand occasion of building new thatched huts that year, he couldn't even force a smile. Spending a day was to delay life for one more day. He was afraid of the arrival of the New Year, which would make his life even more difficult. The beautiful dream was shattered and he couldn't find a trace of it in his mind.

So when he was locked into the county seat with wolf-like chains, he said with a long, roaring laugh to the neighbors who were seeing him off at the village entrance with helpless tears: "Okay! Let's go to the county seat to sit and eat for the New Year!" This tragic story is still considered heroic in the village. But who knew his mood behind the tears!

The old father with a glorious history, since his wife passed away, the dark net has been shrouded in his multi-textured face that has been tortured by work. In the bitter life, he still struggled with his remaining energy to help his son plow a few acres of thin fields, and what was given to him was that the three newly built thatched huts had changed their surname. From then on, he obtained an incurable disease waiting for the day of death to come.

Carrying heavy hardships, Genbao stepped into the dark prison room. No sun, no sympathy. When he was released after mixing up those blurry days, green grass had grown on his father's new grave. So he picked up the iron hoe left by his father again, stepped on the bloodstains left by his father, and lonely planted these few acres of fields that had had glorious days.

He meditated on re-establishing his father's glorious history from his own arms. When the three new thatched huts were built, the family killed sheep and slaughtered pigs, and the old and young people from the neighboring villages all came to congratulate them. On the square, rows of fir tables were lined up, large bowls of meat, large bowls of wine. Mothers often used this lively scene as a story to encourage their sons later. Who in Genbao's village doesn't know? Genbao thought of this glorious history, and beautiful dreams could not help but emerge again.

—Swallows shuttle through the willows, and peasant men sing private love songs in the fields. Genbao ate the lunch sent by his mother, and while his father was smoking a dry marriage and lying under the roots of the tree to rest, he ran to the back of the mountain to mess around with Sister Zhao. Those days, the days of suffering smoothed out

Genbao looked at the neighboring fields, and there was not a single man singing mountain songs. Long fragrant grass grew wildly in the spring breeze. "This is only to starve the peasants!" Gou Fu carried his luggage and didn't know where he went. The warning he left behind made the strong men in the village leave the crops and run to the wharf. Genbao threw the iron hoe beside him, and the fate he was carrying was probably approaching the tomb full of green grass!

The previous generation entrusted their hope to the next generation, and what is the hope of the next generation? The cuckoo bird flew over the treetops. It's time to sow! Spring is not a reading day yesterday's worthless "treasure" mistakenly "treasure owed"

Spring Is Not a Reading Day

Yesterday's Worthless Treasure Mistakenly Treasure Owed

Little White Dove

— Luo Shan

People who work always feel too busy, and people who wander feel too idle, so they think of ways to fill their leisure time. Two weeks ago, a friend sent me a pair of small pigeons. Their feathers were white, their tails were dotted with plum blossoms, and their eyes were exceptionally beautiful. So, the pair of little white pigeons became my companions.

As if driven by a god, early in the morning, around six o'clock, I got out of bed in a panic, opened the window, and slowly peeked at their sleeping faces from the air of the wire mesh, but no matter how early I got up, or how light the footsteps that even I couldn't believe, they were already jumping around there. So I opened the cage door, and they flew away with a flutter.

The cage was placed on the left wall of my three-story building. My house, which is not low, is directly opposite West Lake, and the North Peak is just a straight line. The Eight Characters Pagoda and Gushan are on the right side. The scenery is very beautiful, and it is even more vivid with the embellishment of a pair of small white pigeons.

Caring about the daily life and diet of a pair of small white pigeons, I seemed to have an unspeakable comfort, and that kind of comfort was beyond material and beyond the world.

(Why have I become like this?) I, who have always been annoyed by small creatures, am surprised by the sudden abnormality and often ask myself.

When they flew back tiredly after fluttering their light wings all day, I waited quietly at the window, and then I caught them in my hands, as if to comfort them for their hard work all day. I stroked their feathers, their shiny feathers were of course pleasing, but their warmth was beyond my expectations, and their soft and pretending-to-sleep posture suddenly revealed a natural maternal instinct. I put their eyes on my face, as if they were the only things I cared about and loved.

(Ha! You like them so much, wouldn't it be better if you had children?)

One day, when I was washing them individually, a friend couldn't stand my strange care and said carefully.

(Alas, if it were children, then...)

I swallowed it down. I don't understand why I didn't want to mention those things. Although I have already started to fantasize that if it were children, from the days when I no longer hate small creatures, I would use my whole life to care for them, irrigate them with knowledge, and create ideal great people.

Continuing my daily work, shaking off the bird droppings from the pigeon cage, and putting a new cotton pad underneath, I thought, the sky has been covered with haze for the past few days, and it may snow. If it snows, then this pair of small white pigeons will definitely freeze.

I looked at them squatting in the pigeon cage, my eyebrows were squeezed into three wrinkles, and it felt like a heavy iron block was pressing on my chest.

Paper Kite

— Laborious Heart

Spring has come, and a layer of joy floats in my heart. How should I welcome this spring? Although this spring is not for us.

In my past, full of old traces, I can find examples of how to welcome it, but among these examples, I can never find a good and interesting method, because my past is so ordinary. If I must find one, then I can only say with embarrassment: a paper kite.

Indeed, the paper kite was once my good friend. I remember when I was a five or six-year-old child, a very naughty cattle herder in the countryside. Although life wasn't very good, as a child, as long as there was freedom and friends to play with, I didn't care about anything else. In spring, such a good season, we naughty little comrades were very happy to fly kites. However, our countryside was very remote, and kites were not easy to buy and were very expensive. Therefore, once I didn't succeed in buying a kite, I sulked and didn't eat for a day.

Flying a kite always requires someone's help. I would ask a friend to hold the kite and stand in a high place to lift it up, and then I would hold the string tightly, pulling it with force. If the wind was strong, it would quickly fly high. Sometimes, if the wind was a little calmer, I would stand on the back of an ox to fly it; sometimes, I would even climb onto the roof. When the kite somersaults in the air like a hungry eagle, it can be considered wonderful, but to do this, one must have the skill: those without skill can only watch it fall from high up.

Chinese people like to fight. They can think of ways to fight with anything, and kites are naturally no exception. Therefore, if we accidentally discovered a kite different from our own, we would mobilize our kites very quickly, like discovering an enemy plane during wartime, and surround the enemy until we cut the enemy plane's string with our own string; sometimes, others would cut our kite's string, which would depend on your experience and courage to fight back. I used to enjoy playing this very much because it also required thinking and skill, and it was a more interesting game.

The fleeting past has passed, and now I am drifting into this big city. These pasts can only become historical relics. If we really want to see kite flying, we can only find it in the essays in newspapers and magazines, or see the kite movement promoted by adults and gentlemen to save the country. A few years ago, I saw a poem that described the spring season: "The kite hangs on the power line." This is undoubtedly a good description, but if the author lives in Shanghai, it would be a bit comical. I have never seen a kite flying in the sky in Shanghai.

One day, I accidentally encountered a five or six-year-old child flying a kite on the road. I felt a little happy in my heart: my ideal is not necessarily correct, there are also children flying kites in big cities. But when I saw the child's pitiful appearance of flying a kite, I couldn't help but feel disappointed, because he was so stupid. On a road covered with coal smoke and ash, a half-broken kite was flying on the small string he was pulling, perhaps not even able to fly over an adult's head. Such flying is useless; I almost wanted to help him make his kite fly higher. But undoubtedly, this is also an ideal. No matter how skilled you are, you cannot make a broken kite fly into the sky in such a flat, crowded place. ...

Ah—I was frightened. The little child, the little child flying the kite, was knocked down by a car. Crying on the ground.

Spring may not come to our domain, perhaps.

Spring Rain

— Chen Liang

Opening that dark green window curtain didn't reveal a morning illuminated by cheerful and warm sunlight as usual, but rather, a gloomy day that made everyone who saw it feel uncomfortable.

"It's going to rain, the sky never wants to give people a few more refreshing days!"

With unkempt hair and arms wrapped tightly around her purple-red pajamas, she lay down on the sofa, her face as gloomy as the weather, not wanting to laugh but also not wanting to cry. She had lived through yesterday, and she was thinking about today... today?

But, on the half of the bed, there was someone sleeping on their side, face outward, with half a "White Gold Dragon" cigarette stuck to their lips, a young man calling her name—continuously; "Cai'e... Cai'e..."

It really started to rain, tapping on the glass window, continuous—spring rain.

She didn't reply, only using her right hand to hit her own head. Who is calling this name? For the sake of life, even her age and name must be hidden from people, why? I am deceiving people all my life to survive in the world, why can't I say my real surname and age? She was so angry that she really wanted to cry sadly, but it was absolutely impossible. Tears should be swallowed into her stomach. In this position, she only has the duty to laugh, not the right to cry. She turned over and fell into the abyss of bottomless sorrow.

"Do you have a headache?" the young man lying on the bed asked, with a hint of strange light in his eyes.

"Thank you, this kind of false affection, this kind of hypocritical, insincere concern. You didn't come for love, you came for lust. Don't say headache, even if I suddenly die today, you would still go your way—" she thought. She deliberately ignored him. She understood her own situation and position better than anyone else, but she couldn't directly point out the hypocrisy of a man who would give her some life source under certain conditions.

The rain outside the window was getting heavier and heavier, "Hua Hua Hua Hua," like it would never stop. Several parallel power lines were also endlessly shedding tears into the window. Each raindrop hit the glass windowpane, also hitting

Page 20

Page 21

hitting her tender heart, arousing stars of old creation hidden pain, slowly spreading and elusive - nerve pain.

The young man got out of bed and came over, using his rough hands to twist her head, like a plaster bust displayed in an art academy, not wanting to laugh or cry.

"Swallow a few aspirin."

"Why?"

"Don't you have headaches!"

But she laughed, "Illness! Do you understand my illness? Can aspirin cure my illness?" Such a loud voice sprayed out from her purple-red lips. She reached out and brushed aside the messy hair hanging in front of her eyes, and ran to the window in one breath. Rain and wind were attacking her through a thin piece of glass. She looked at the city streets below through the misty air, still rushing back and forth, with busy pedestrians and streetcars appearing at every moment.
